It handles various error cases such as out-of-order samples,\\n1297: // out-of-bounds samples, and too-old samples, updating the appenderCommitContext accordingly.\\n1298: //\\n1299: // For out-of-order samples, it checks if the sample can be inserted into the series and updates\\n1300: // the out-of-order mmap markers if necessary. (2) A float sample was appended to this\\n1326: \\t\\t\\t// series before via this same appender.\\n1327: \\t\\t\\t//\\n1328: \\t\\t\\t// In either case, we need to check the previous sample\\n1329: \\t\\t\\t// in the memSeries to append the appropriately typed\\n1330: \\t\\t\\t// staleness marker.
